								<div class="component-content">
	                            	<article class="item-page" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">

<div itemprop="articleBody">
<!-- <div class="sectionImageModule" style="padding-top:8px;"> -->
<!-- 	<img src="https://wildlife.utah.gov/i/stocking_reports_head.png" class="scaleMobile" alt="Stocking reports"> -->
<!-- </div> -->
<!-- Jan 3rd 2013 - AHeyman - Made changes so year worked with sorting.   -->


	<link rel="stylesheet" href="css/FishStocking.css" type="text/css">
	<SCRIPT type="text/javascript">
	var originalList;
	var clicked = "";
	var sortOrder = "ASC";
	var prevOrder = "watername";
	var specific = "";
	var sortSpecific = "ALL";
	// clickedWhat will have 4 possible values, label, watername, county or species
	function newSort(clickedWhat, order){
		// alert (clickedWhat + "X" + order);
		if ( clickedWhat == "label" ) {
			prevOrder = order;
			sortSpecific = "ALL";
			specific = "";
			if (clicked == order) {
				sortOrder = "DESC";
				clicked = "";
			} else {
				sortOrder = "ASC";
				clicked = order;
			}
		} else {
			clicked = "";
			if (specific == order) {
				sortSpecific = "ALL";
				specific = order;
			} else {
				sortSpecific = order;
				specific = "";
			}
		}
		var xmlhttp;
		if (window.XMLHttpRequest) { // code for IE7+, Firefox, Chrome, Opera, Safari
			xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
		} else { // code for IE6, IE5
			xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
		}

		xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
			if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4 && xmlhttp.status == 200) {
				document.getElementById("fishTableBody").innerHTML = xmlhttp.responseText;
// 				$("#fishTable").innerHTML = xmlhttp.responseText;
				// console.log(xmlhttp.responseText);
				jQuery("#fishTable").trigger("update");
			}
		}
		// change to include year
		// xmlhttp.open("GET", "report2.jsp?sort=" + prevOrder + "&sortorder="
		xmlhttp.open("GET", "FishAjax?y=" + 2024 + "&sort=" + prevOrder + "&sortorder="		
				+ sortOrder + "&sortspecific=" + sortSpecific + "&whichSpecific=" + clickedWhat, true);
		xmlhttp.send();
		// document.getElementById("resetbutton").disabled = false;
		document.getElementById("resetbutton").style.visibility = "visible";
	}
	
	function resetDisplay() {
		document.getElementById("fishTableBody").innerHTML = originalList;
		jQuery("#fishTable").trigger("update");
		// document.getElementById("resetbutton").disabled = true;
		document.getElementById("resetbutton").style.visibility = "hidden";
	}
	
	window.onload = function() {
		console.log("onload happening");
		// Disabled 4/18/2019 for new wildlife server ... work on fixing.
		jQuery("#fishTable").tablesorter();
		originalList = document.getElementById("fishTableBody").innerHTML;
		// console.log("onload");
		console.log("onload list", originalList);
		document.getElementById("resetbutton").style.visibility = "hidden";
	}
	</SCRIPT>
	<div id="sortArea">

		<p id=instructions>Click a column label to sort by that column.  Click again to reverse the sort order.<br />
			You can also click items in the table to see specific <i>waters</i>, <i>counties</i> or <i>species</i>.<br />
		    Please be patient it might take a few moments to process.</p>
		<input id="resetbutton" type="button" onclick="resetDisplay()" value="Display All" class="button1"></input> 
		<div id="reset"></div>
		</div>
	</div>
